Having proved a preservation property in the last chapter, a natural
next step would be to prove progress. That is, to prove a property
of the form

    If Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v, then either M is a lambda abstraction or M â€”â†’ N for some N.

Such a property would tell us that having a denotation implies either
reduction to normal form or divergence. This is indeed true, but we
can prove a much stronger property! In fact, having a denotation that
is a function value (not `âŠ¥`) implies reduction to a lambda
abstraction (no divergence).

This stronger property, reformulated a bit, is known as _adequacy_.
That is, if a term `M` is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then `M` reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    â„° M â‰ƒ â„° (Æ› N)  implies M â€”â†  Æ› N' for some N'

Recall that `â„° M â‰ƒ â„° (Æ› N)` is equivalent to saying that
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` for some `v` and `w`. We will show that
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` implies reduction a lambda abstraction.

It is well known that a term can reduce to a lambda abstraction using
full Î² reduction if and only if it can reduce to a lambda abstraction
using the call-by-name reduction strategy. So we shall prove that
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` implies that `M` halts under call-by-name evaluation,
which we define with a big-step semantics written `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c`, where
`c` is a closure (a term paired with an environment) and `Î³'` is an
environment that maps variables to closures

So we will show that `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (v â†¦ w)` implies `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c`,
provided `Î³` and `Î³'` are appropriate related.  The proof will
be an induction on the derivation of `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, and to
strengthen the induction hypothesis, we will relate semantic values to
closures using a _logical relation_ `ğ•`.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* We loosen the requirement that `M` result in a function value and
  instead require that `M` result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the call-by-name big-step semantics of the lambda calculus
  and prove that it is deterministic.

* We define the logical relation `ğ•` that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms `ğ”¼` and environments `ğ”¾`.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'` and `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, then `ğ”¼ v (clos M Î³')`.

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.


## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

If a value `u` is greater than a function, then an even greater value `u'`
is too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun-âŠ‘"></a><a id="3836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3836" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ‘</a> <a id="3847" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3849" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="3851" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3851" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="3853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3853" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="3856" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="3863" class="Symbol">}</a>

The bottom value `âŠ¥` is not greater than a function.

If the join of two values `u` and `u'` is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

On the other hand, if neither of `u` and `u'` is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-âŠ”"></a><a id="4915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4915" class="Function">not-AboveFun-âŠ”</a> <a id="4930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4932" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="4934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4934" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4936" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="4939" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4946" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="4963" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="4965" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="4967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3651" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4934" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4978" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="4980" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="4982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3651" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4936" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
               <a id="5009" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="5011" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="5013" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3651" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5022" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4934" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŠ”</a> <a id="5027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4936" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5029" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4915" class="Function">not-AboveFun-âŠ”</a> <a id="5046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5046" class="Bound">naf1</a> <a id="5051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5051" class="Bound">naf2</a> <a id="5056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5056" class="Bound">af12</a>
    <a id="5065" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="5070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4402" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ”</a> <a id="5081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5056" class="Bound">af12</a>
<a id="5086" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5090" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5092" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚</a> <a id="5097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5097" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5101" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5103" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5097" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5121" class="Bound">naf1</a>
<a id="5126" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5130" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5132" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚‚</a> <a id="5137" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5137" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5141" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5143" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5137" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5161" class="Bound">naf2</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-âŠ”-inv"></a><a id="5308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5308" class="Function">not-AboveFun-âŠ”-inv</a> <a id="5327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5329" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="5331" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5331" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5333" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5343" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5345" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="5347" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">Â¬</a> <a id="5349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3651" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5358" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5331" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŠ”</a> <a id="5363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5333" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5365" class="Symbol">)</a>

The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

## Big-step semantics for call-by-name lambda calculus

To better align with the denotational semantics, we shall use an
environment-passing big-step semantics. Because this is call-by-name,
an environment maps each variable to a closure, that is, to a term
paired with its environment. (Environments and closures are mutually
recursive.) We define environments and closures as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ClosEnv"></a><a id="6669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6677" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2980" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="6687" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6689" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

<a id="6694" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Clos"></a><a id="6699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="6704" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6706" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6710" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Clos.clos"></a><a id="6718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6718" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="6723" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6725" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="6727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6727" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="6728" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6730" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6732" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6733" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6735" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6727" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="6741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="6742" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6744" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6727" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6756" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a>

<a id="6764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6772" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6772" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6774" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6776" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="6778" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6779" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6781" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6772" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">âˆ‹</a> <a id="6787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="6788" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6790" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6792" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As usual, we have the empty environment, and we can extend an
environment.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="âˆ…&#39;"></a><a id="6897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6897" class="Function">âˆ…&#39;</a> <a id="6900" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6910" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">âˆ…</a>

<a id="_,&#39;_"></a><a id="6919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6919" class="Function Operator">_,&#39;_</a> <a id="6924" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6926" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="6928" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6929" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="6930" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6932" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6929" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6944" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6946" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="6951" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6953" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6929" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="6964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="6967" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="6969" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6970" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="6972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6919" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="6975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6975" class="Bound">c</a><a id="6976" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="6980" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6975" class="Bound">c</a>
<a id="6984" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6985" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="6987" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6919" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="6990" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6990" class="Bound">c</a><a id="6991" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6993" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="6996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6996" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6997" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6999" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6985" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="7003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6996" class="Bound">x</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The following is the big-step semantics for call-by-name evaluation,
which we describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7125" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_âŠ¢_â‡“_"></a><a id="7130" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7130" class="Datatype Operator">_âŠ¢_â‡“_</a> <a id="7136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7138" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="7140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7140" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="7141" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7143" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="7153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7140" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="7155" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7157" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7140" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="7160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="7162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="7163" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7165" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7172" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7174" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7178" class="Keyword">where</a>

       <a id="7513" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7515" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7442" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="7517" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7473" class="Bound">Î´</a> <a id="7545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link          <a id="7575" class="Comment">----------------------------------------------------</a>
       <a id="7635" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7442" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="7639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7130" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="7641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7457" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="7643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Â·</a> <a id="7645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7459" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7130" class="Datatype Operator">â‡“</a> <a id="7649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7503" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* The `â‡“-var` rule evaluates a variable by finding the associated
  closure in the environment and then evaluating the closure.

* The `â‡“-lam` rule turns a lambda abstraction into a closure
  by packaging it up with its environment.

* The `â‡“-app` rule performs function application by first evaluating
  the term `L` in operator position. If that produces a closure containing
  a lambda abstraction `Æ› N`, then we evaluate the body `N` in an
  environment extended with the argument `M`. Note that `M` is not
  evaluated in rule `â‡“-app` because this is call-by-name and not
  call-by-value.

If the big-step semantics says that a term `M` evaluates to both `c` and
`c'`, then `c` and `c'` are identical. In other words, the big-step relation
is a partial function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="â‡“-determ"></a><a id="8444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8444" class="Function">â‡“-determ</a> <a id="8453" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8455" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="8457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8457" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="8458" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8460" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8460" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="8462" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="8472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8457" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="8473" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8475" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8475" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8477" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8479" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8457" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="8481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="8483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="8484" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8486" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8488" class="Bound">c&#39;</a> <a id="8491" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8493" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="8497" class="Symbol">}</a>

## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation `ğ•` is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction, i.e., in weak-head normal
form (WHNF). The relation ğ”¼ is for any closure. Roughly speaking,
`ğ”¼ v c` will hold if, when `v` is greater than a function value, `c` evaluates
to a closure `c'` in WHNF and `ğ• v c'`. Regarding `ğ• v c`, it will hold when
`c` is in WHNF, and if `v` is a function, the body of `c` evaluates
according to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ğ•"></a><a id="9284" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9284" class="Function">ğ•</a> <a id="9286" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9288" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="9294" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9296" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="9301" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9303" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="ğ”¼"></a><a id="9307" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9307" class="Function">ğ”¼</a> <a id="9309" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="9317" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6699" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="9324" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9326" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We define `ğ•` as a function from values and closures to `Set` and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with `ğ”¼` in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then `ğ•` is false (`Bot`). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define `ğ•` by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

class="Bound">N</a><a id="10009" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9990" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="10012" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10014" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">Ã—</a> <a id="10016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9284" class="Function">ğ•</a> <a id="10018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9975" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6718" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10026" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Æ›</a> <a id="10029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9987" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10030" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9990" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="10033" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* If the value is `âŠ¥`, then the result is true (`âŠ¤`).

* If the value is a join (u âŠ” v), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of ğ• is true for both u and v.

* The important case is for a function value `v â†¦ w` and closure
  `clos (Æ› N) Î³`. Given any closure `c` such that `ğ”¼ v c`, if `w` is
  greater than a function, then `N` evaluates (with `Î³` extended with `c`)
  to some closure `c'` and we have `ğ• w c'`.


The definition of `ğ”¼` is straightforward. If `v` is a greater than a
function, then `M` evaluates to a closure related to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9307" class="Function">ğ”¼</a> <a id="10611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10621" class="Bound">Î³&#39;</a><a id="10623" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10625" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3651" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="10636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10611" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10638" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="10640" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Î£[</a> <a id="10643" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10671" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10643" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the main lemma is by induction on `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). So we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, `ğ”¾`
relates `Î³` to `Î³'` if the corresponding values and closures are related
by `ğ”¼`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ğ”¾"></a><a id="11051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11051" class="Function">ğ”¾</a> <a id="11053" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11055" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="11057" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11057" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="11058" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11060" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="11066" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11057" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11068" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6669" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="11078" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11057" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11080" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11082" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

We need a few properties of the `ğ•` and `ğ”¼` relations.  The first is that
a closure in the `ğ•` relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11503" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="11508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11508" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="11513" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11515" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="11517" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11518" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11520" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11520" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11521" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11523" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11518" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="11529" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11520" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11531" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11533" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="11537" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.Æ›_"></a><a id="11545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11545" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Æ›_</a> <a id="11548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11550" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="11552" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11553" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="11554" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11556" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11557" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11557" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="11559" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11553" class="Bound">Î“</a> <a id="11563" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11565" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a> <a id="11567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">âŠ¢</a> <a id="11569" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">â˜…</a><a id="11570" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="11577" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11508" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="11584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">Æ›</a> <a id="11587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11557" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11588" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

Next we have an introduction rule for `ğ•` that mimics the `âŠ”-intro`
rule. If both `u` and `v` are related to a closure `c`, then their join is
too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ğ•âŠ”-intro"></a><a id="11997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11997" class="Function">ğ•âŠ”-intro</a> <a id="12006" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12008" class="Symbol">âˆ€{</a><a id="12010" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12010" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="12012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12012" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="12014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12014" class="Bound">v</a><a id="12015" class="Symbol">}</a>

           <a id="12053" class="Comment">---------------</a>

In a moment we prove that `ğ•` is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if `ğ• v c` and `v' âŠ‘ v`, then `ğ• v' c`.
This property, named `ğ•-sub`, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the `sub` rule.

To prove `ğ•-sub`, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to `âŠ¥`. In such cases, `ğ• v (clos (Æ› N) Î³')` is trivially true.

The proofs of `ğ•-sub` and `ğ”¼-sub` are intertwined.

We prove `ğ•-sub` by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
`v' âŠ‘ v`. We describe each case below.

<a id="15000" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="15004" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15006" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚</a> <a id="15011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15011" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="15015" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15017" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">âŠ¥-elim</a> <a id="15024" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15025" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="15039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15011" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="15043" class="Bound">naf2</a><a id="15047" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15049" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="15053" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15055" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">injâ‚‚</a> <a id="15060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15060" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="15064" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15066" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">âŠ¥-elim</a> <a id="15073" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15074" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="15088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15060" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="15092" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="15096" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `BotâŠ‘`. We immediately have `ğ• âŠ¥ (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `ConjLâŠ‘`.

        vâ‚' âŠ‘ v     vâ‚‚' âŠ‘ v
        -------------------
        (vâ‚' âŠ” vâ‚‚') âŠ‘ v

  The induction hypotheses gives us `ğ• vâ‚' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`
  and `ğ• vâ‚‚' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`, which is all we need for this case. 

* Case `ConjR1âŠ‘`.

        v' âŠ‘ vâ‚
        -------------
        v' âŠ‘ (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)

  The induction hypothesis gives us `ğ• v' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `ConjR2âŠ‘`.

        v' âŠ‘ vâ‚‚
        -------------
        v' âŠ‘ (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us `ğ• v' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `TransâŠ‘`.

        v' âŠ‘ vâ‚‚   vâ‚‚ âŠ‘ v
        -----------------
             v' âŠ‘ v

  The induction hypothesis for `vâ‚‚ âŠ‘ v` gives us
  `ğ• vâ‚‚ (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  for `v' âŠ‘ vâ‚‚` to conclude that `ğ• v' (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`.

* Case `DistâŠ‘`. This case  is the most difficult. We have

        ğ• (v â†¦ w) (clos (Æ› N) Î³)
        ğ• (v â†¦ w') (clos (Æ› N) Î³)

  and need to show that 

        ğ• (v â†¦ (w âŠ” w')) (clos (Æ› N) Î³)
  
  Let `c` be an arbtrary closure such that `ğ”¼ v c`.
  Assume `w âŠ” w'` is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both `w` and `w'`
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma `AboveFun-âŠ”`,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.
  
  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    `Î³ âŠ¢ N â‡“ clos L Î´` and `ğ• w (clos L Î´)`.  We also have `Î³ âŠ¢ N â‡“ câ‚ƒ` and
    `ğ• w' câ‚ƒ`.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    `câ‚ƒ â‰¡ clos L Î´`. Also, from `ğ• w (clos L Î´)` we know that `L â‰¡ Æ› N'`
    for some `N'`. We conclude that `ğ• (w âŠ” w') (clos (Æ› N') Î´)`.

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say `AboveFun w` and `Â¬ AboveFun w'`. Then from
    `ğ• (v â†¦ w) (clos (Æ› N) Î³)`
    we have `Î³ âŠ¢ N â‡“ clos L Î³â‚` and `ğ• w (clos L Î³â‚)`. From this we have
    `L â‰¡ Æ› N'` for some `N'`. Meanwhile, from `Â¬ AboveFun w'` we have
    `ğ• w' (clos L Î³â‚)`. We conclude that
    `ğ• (w âŠ” w') (clos (Æ› N') Î³â‚)`.
    

The proof of `sub-ğ”¼` is direct and explained below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#13157" class="Function">sub-ğ”¼</a> <a id="17229" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6718" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="17235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17235" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="17237" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17237" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="17238" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17240" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17241" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17241" class="Bound">v</a><a id="17242" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17244" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17245" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="17247" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17249" class="Bound">ğ”¼v</a> <a id="17252" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17252" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a> <a id="17257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17257" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="17265" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="17270" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17249" class="Bound">ğ”¼v</a> <a id="17273" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3836" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ‘</a> <a id="17285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17257" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="17289" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17252" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a><a id="17293" class="Symbol">)</a>

From `AboveFun v'` and `v' âŠ‘ v` we have `AboveFun v`.  Then with `ğ”¼ v c` we
obtain a closure `c` such that `Î³ âŠ¢ M â‡“ c` and `ğ• v c`. We conclude with an
application of `sub-ğ•` with `v' âŠ‘ v` to show `ğ• v' c`.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. More formally, if
`Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v` and `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'`, then `ğ”¼ v (clos M Î³')`. The proof is by
induction on the derivation of `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v` we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the `var` rule.

    <a id="20269" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="20274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18244" class="Function">â†“â†’ğ”¼</a> <a id="20278" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20215" class="Bound">Î“</a><a id="20280" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20282" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20219" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="20284" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20223" class="Bound">Î³&#39;</a><a id="20289" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20291" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20228" class="Bound">M</a><a id="20293" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20295" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20236" class="Bound">ğ”¾Î³Î³&#39;</a> <a id="20300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20253" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="20302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20303" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3836" class="Function">AboveFun-âŠ‘</a> <a id="20314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20261" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="20318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20255" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a><a id="20322" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="20324" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="20328" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="20330" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20332" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20332" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="20334" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20336" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20338" class="Bound">Mâ‡“c</a> <a id="20342" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20344" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20344" class="Bound">ğ•v</a> <a id="20347" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a> <a id="20349" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a> <a id="20351" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="20359" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20332" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="20363" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20365" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ¨</a> <a id="20367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20338" class="Bound">Mâ‡“c</a> <a id="20371" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#13105" class="Function">sub-ğ•</a> <a id="20379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20344" class="Bound">ğ•v</a> <a id="20382" class="Bound">v&#39;âŠ‘v</a> <a id="20387" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a> <a id="20389" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âŸ©</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `var`. Looking up `x` in `Î³'` yields some closure, `clos M' Î´`,
  and from `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'` we have `ğ”¼ (Î³ x) (clos M' Î´)`. With the premise
  `AboveFun (Î³ x)`, we obtain a closure `c` such that `Î´ âŠ¢ M' â‡“ c`
  and `ğ• (Î³ x) c`. To conclude `Î³' âŠ¢ x â‡“ c` via `â‡“-var`, we 
  need `Î³' x â‰¡ clos M' Î´`, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the `kth-x` lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case `â†¦-elim`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ L Â· M â†“ v`.
  The induction hypothesis for `Î³ âŠ¢ L â†“ vâ‚ â†¦ v`
  gives us `Î³' âŠ¢ L â‡“ clos L' Î´` and `ğ• v (clos L' Î´)`.
  Of course, `L' â‰¡ Æ› N` for some `N`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚`,
  we have `ğ”¼ vâ‚ (clos M Î³')`.
  Together with the premise `AboveFun v` and `ğ• v (clos L' Î´)`,
  we obtain a closure `c'` such that `Î´ âŠ¢ N â‡“ c'` and `ğ• v c'`.
  We conclude that `Î³' âŠ¢ L Â· M â‡“ c'` by rule `â‡“-app`.

* Case `â†¦-intro`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ Æ› N â†“ v â†¦ w`.
  We immediately have `Î³' âŠ¢ Æ› M â‡“ clos (Æ› M) Î³'` by rule `â‡“-lam`.
  But we also need to prove `ğ• (v â†¦ w) (clos (Æ› N) Î³')`.
  Let `c` by an arbitrary closure such that `ğ”¼ v c`.
  Suppose `v'` is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that `Î³' , c âŠ¢ N â‡“ c'` and `ğ• v' c'` for some `c'`.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for `Î³ , v âŠ¢ N â†“ v'`
  but we must first show that `ğ”¾ (Î³ , v) (Î³' , c)`. We prove
  that by the lemma `ğ”¾-ext`, using facts `ğ”¾ Î³ Î³'` and `ğ”¼ v c`.

* Case `âŠ¥-intro`. We have the premise `AboveFun âŠ¥`, but that's impossible.

* Case `âŠ”-intro`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)` and `AboveFun (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚)`
  and need to show `Î³' âŠ¢ M â†“ c` and `ğ• (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚) c` for some `c`.
  Again, by `AboveFun-âŠ”`, at least one of `vâ‚` or `vâ‚‚` is greater than
  a function.

  * Suppose both `vâ‚` and `vâ‚‚` are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚` and `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚‚`
    we have `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ câ‚`, `ğ• vâ‚ câ‚`, `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ câ‚‚`, and `ğ• vâ‚‚ câ‚‚`
    for some `câ‚` and `câ‚‚`. Because `â‡“` is deterministic, we have `câ‚‚ â‰¡ câ‚`.
    Then by `ğ•âŠ”-intro` we conclude that `ğ• (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚) câ‚`.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose `vâ‚` is greater than a function
    value but `vâ‚‚` is not.  By the induction hypotheses for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ vâ‚`,
    and using `ğ•â†’WHNF`, we have `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚`
    and `ğ• vâ‚ (clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚)`.
    Then because `vâ‚‚` is not greater than a function, we also have
    `ğ• vâ‚‚ (clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚)`. We conclude that `ğ• (vâ‚ âŠ” vâ‚‚) (clos (Æ› N) Î³â‚)`.
    
* Case `sub`. We have `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v`, `v' âŠ‘ v`, and `AboveFun v'`.
  We need to show that `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c` and `ğ• v' c` for some `c`.
  We have `AboveFun v` by `AboveFun-âŠ‘`,
  so the induction hypothesis for `Î³ âŠ¢ M â†“ v` gives us a closure `c`
  such that `Î³' âŠ¢ M â‡“ c` and `ğ• v c`. We conclude that `ğ• v' c` by `sub-ğ•`.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

The adequacy property is a corollary of the main lemma.
We have `âˆ… âŠ¢ Æ› N â†“ âŠ¥ â†¦ âŠ¥`, so `â„° M â‰ƒ â„° (Æ› N)`
gives us `âˆ… âŠ¢ M â†“ âŠ¥ â†¦ âŠ¥`. Then the main lemma gives us
`âˆ… âŠ¢ M â‡“ clos (Æ› Nâ€²) Î³` for some `Nâ€²` and `Î³`.
